    \hypertarget{cross-check-mu_star-error}{%
\section{\texorpdfstring{Cross-Check: \(\mu_{\star}\)
Error}{Cross-Check: \textbackslash{}mu\_\{\textbackslash{}star\} Error}}\label{cross-check-mu_star-error}}

We want to verify if the \(\mu_{\star}\) error are consistent. For
instance, they seem to be pretty large.

    \hypertarget{plot-mu_star-error}{%
\subsection{\texorpdfstring{Plot \(\mu_{\star}\)
Error}{Plot \textbackslash{}mu\_\{\textbackslash{}star\} Error}}\label{plot-mu_star-error}}

This error was computed by a jackniffe techinique.

\begin{verbatim}

def jackknife_var(x, func):
    """Jackknife estiamte of the variance of the estimator func."""
    n = len(x)
    idx = np.arange(n)
    j_est = jackknife(x, func)
    return (n-1)/(n + 0.0) * np.sum((func(x[idx!=i]) - j_est)**2.0 for i in range(n))
\end{verbatim}

The stellar mass errors was not taken into account

\begin{verbatim}
linear_mass_weight = pmem*10**mass
mu_star_err_jk = (jackknife_var(linear_mass_weight, lambda_star_jk))**0.5
\end{verbatim}

\end{Verbatim}
